            var googletag = googletag || {};

            googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

            window.onload = function () {

                var ads = document.querySelectorAll("[data-advert]");

                if (ads !== null && ads.length > 0) {

                    (function () {

                        var gads = document.createElement('script');

                        gads.async = true;

                        gads.type = 'text/javascript';

                        var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;

                        gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';

                        var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];

                        node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);

                    })();

                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {

                        var toDisplay = [];

                        var fromJP = $('#From');                            

                        var toJP = $('#To');  



                        function addDisplayAd(ad, id) {

                            var sc = document.createElement('script');

                            sc.type = 'text/javascript';

                            sc.text = "googletag.cmd.push(function () { googletag.display('" + id + "'); });";

                            ad.appendChild(sc);

                        }

            

                        for (var i = 0; i < ads.length; i++) {

                            var ad = ads[i];

                            if (ad.offsetParent === null) {

                                continue;

                            }

                            var id = 'adv-' + i;

                            var path = ad.getAttribute("data-advert");

                            var sizesArr = ad.getAttribute("data-advert-sizes").split('|');

                            var sizes = [];

                            for (var s = 0; s < sizesArr.length; s++) {

                                sizes.push(sizesArr[s].split(',').map(Number));

                            }

                            addDisplayAd(ad, id);

                            toDisplay.push(id);

                            ad.setAttribute("id", id);

                            googletag.defineSlot(path, sizes, id).addService(googletag.pubads());

                        }



                        if (fromJP.val() !== "" && toJP.val() !== "") {

                            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('from', fromJP);

                            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('to', toJP);

                        } 



                        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

                        googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);

                        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);

                        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {



                            if (!event.isEmpty) {                                

                                var child = $('#' + event.slot.getSlotElementId());

                                var adLabel = '<a class="advertisement-label" href="/info-for/business-and-commercial/commercial-opportunities/advertising-on-the-network">Advertisement</a>';



                                if (child.parent().hasClass("advert-content")) {

                                    child.append(adLabel).closest('.advert-link').css('background', '#f7f7f7');

                                } else {

                                    child.prepend(adLabel);

                                }

                            }

                        });

                        googletag.enableServices();

                        for (var ii = 0; ii < toDisplay.length; ii++) {

                            googletag.display(toDisplay[ii]);

                        }

                    });

                }

            };

        </script>

        <script type='text/javascript'>

            var googletag = googletag || {};

            googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];

            window.onload = function () {

                var ads = document.querySelectorAll("[data-advert]");

                if (ads !== null && ads.length > 0) {

                    (function () {

                        var gads = document.createElement('script');

                        gads.async = true;

                        gads.type = 'text/javascript';

                        var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;

                        gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';

                        var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];

                        node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);

                    })();

                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {

                        var toDisplay = [];

                        var fromJP = $('#From');                            

                        var toJP = $('#To');  



                        function addDisplayAd(ad, id) {

                            var sc = document.createElement('script');

                            sc.type = 'text/javascript';

                            sc.text = "googletag.cmd.push(function () { googletag.display('" + id + "'); });";

                            ad.appendChild(sc);

                        }

            

                        for (var i = 0; i < ads.length; i++) {

                            var ad = ads[i];

                            if (ad.offsetParent === null) {

                                continue;

                            }

                            var id = 'adv-' + i;

                            var path = ad.getAttribute("data-advert");

                            var sizesArr = ad.getAttribute("data-advert-sizes").split('|');

                            var sizes = [];

                            for (var s = 0; s < sizesArr.length; s++) {

                                sizes.push(sizesArr[s].split(',').map(Number));

                            }

                            addDisplayAd(ad, id);

                            toDisplay.push(id);

                            ad.setAttribute("id", id);

                            googletag.defineSlot(path, sizes, id).addService(googletag.pubads());

                        }



                        if (fromJP.val() !== "" && toJP.val() !== "") {

                            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('from', fromJP);

                            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('to', toJP);

                        } 



                        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();

                        googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);

                        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);

                        googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {



                            if (!event.isEmpty) {                                

                                var child = $('#' + event.slot.getSlotElementId());

                                var adLabel = '<a class="advertisement-label" href="/info-for/business-and-commercial/commercial-opportunities/advertising-on-the-network">Advertisement</a>';



                                if (child.parent().hasClass("advert-content")) {

                                    child.append(adLabel).closest('.advert-link').css('background', '#f7f7f7');

                                } else {

                                    child.prepend(adLabel);

                                }

                            }

                        });

                        googletag.enableServices();

                        for (var ii = 0; ii < toDisplay.length; ii++) {

                            googletag.display(toDisplay[ii]);

                        }

                    });

                }

            };

        </script>
